                                  Approval of ITU-T Recommendations
By AAP-53, it was announced that the following ITU-T Recommendations were approved, in accordance with the
procedures outlined in Recommendation ITU-T A.8:
–     ITU-T F.740.8 (06/2024): Requirements and architecture for live virtual tour system using panoramic video and
      augmented reality
–     ITU-T F.743.25 (06/2024): Procedures and requirements for multimedia data asset management
–     ITU-T F.743.26 (06/2024): Technical requirements of cloud gaming platform based on IMT-2020 mobile edge
      computing
–     ITU-T F.746.18 (06/2024): Requirements for interactive low-latency multimedia transmission system over the
      Internet
–     ITU-T F.747.14 (06/2024): Requirements and capability framework of the multimodal fusion system for vision
–     ITU-T F.747.15 (06/2024): Requirements of event-based vision systems
–     ITU-T F.748.28 (06/2024): Requirements and functional architecture of digital twin platform for supporting
      multimedia services
–     ITU-T F.748.29 (06/2024): Framework and requirements of computer audition based machinery fault diagnosis
      systems
–     ITU-T F.748.30 (06/2024): Requirements of communication services for digital humans
–     ITU-T F.748.34 (06/2024): Requirements for the construction of multimedia knowledge graph database structure
      based on artificial intelligence
–     ITU-T F.748.35 (06/2024): Requirement and framework of trustworthy federated machine learning based service
–     ITU-T F.748.36 (06/2024): Requirements and framework of multi-algorithm scheduling systems
–     ITU-T F.748.37 (06/2024): Requirements and functional framework of joint semantic query system of unstructured
      data across clusters
–     ITU-T F.748.38 (06/2024): Technical specification for artificial intelligence cloud platform: General architecture
–     ITU-T F.749.18 (06/2024): Framework and requirements for emergency services using civilian unmanned aerial
      vehicles
–     ITU-T F.751.14 (06/2024): Reference architecture for information tracing of renewable energy consumption based
      on distributed ledger technology
–     ITU-T F.751.15 (06/2024): Assessment methods for distributed ledger technology (DLT) management service
      platforms
–     ITU-T F.751.16 (06/2024): Reference framework for distributed ledger technology (DLT) management service
      platforms
–     ITU-T F.751.17 (06/2024): Smart contract lifecycle management requirements for distributed ledger technology
      systems
–     ITU-T F.751.18 (06/2024): Framework for DLT-based energy metering data sharing
–     ITU-T F.751.19 (06/2024): Framework and requirements for distributed ledger technology based on sharding
      technique
–     ITU-T F.751.20 (06/2024): Reference architecture for DLT-based multimedia data delivery management systems
–     ITU-T F.751.21 (06/2024): Technical Requirements on inter-chain interoperability for permissioned distributed
      ledger technologies
–     ITU-T F.751.22 (06/2024): Financial distributed ledger technology application guideline
–     ITU-T F.781.1 (06/2024): General framework of quality control of medical images for machine learning applications
–     ITU-T F.781.2 (06/2024): Quality assessment requirements for artificial intelligence/machine learning-based
      software as a medical device
–     ITU-T H.266.2 (V2) (06/2024): Reference software for ITU-T H.266 versatile video coding

–   ITU-T H.430.8 (06/2024): Functional architecture of interactive immersive services (IIS) systems
–   ITU-T H.626.7 (06/2024): Functional architecture for machine vision systems in smart manufacturing

Communication of 13.VI.2024:

                                  Granting of Recognized Operating Agency (ROA) status
The Instituto Federal de Telecomunicaciones (IFT), Ciudad de México, announces that the following telecommunication
operator and service provider has been granted the status of Recognized Operating Agency (ROA), in accordance with
Article 6 of, and Nos. 1007 and 1008 of the Annex to, the Constitution of ITU.
The name of the telecommunication operator and service provider to which the status of Recognized Operating Agency
(ROA) has been granted, is: Pantera Mobile Solutions S.A.P.I. de C.V.

                                         National Numbering Plan
                          (According to Recommendation ITU-T E.129 (01/2013))
                                                Web: www.itu.int/itu-t/inr/nnp/index.html
Administrations are requested to notify ITU about their national numbering plan changes, or to give an explanation on
their webpage concerning the national numbering plan as well as their contact points, so that the information, which will
be made available freely to all administrations/ROAs and service providers, can be posted on the ITU-T website.
For their numbering website, or when sending their information to ITU/TSB (e-mail: tsbtson@itu.int), administrations are
kindly requested to use the format as explained in Recommendation ITU-T E.129. They are reminded that they will be
responsible for the timely update of this information.
From 1.VI.2024, the following countries/geographical areas have updated their national numbering plan on our site:

Geneva, 2024
           List of International Signalling Point Codes (ISPC)


Note from TSB


1.      This List of International Signalling Point Codes (ISPC) replaces the previous one published as Annex to
the ITU Operational Bulletin No. 1199 of 1.VII.2020. Since then, a number of notifications have been received
at TSB and they have been published separately in various issues of the ITU Operational Bulletin. The present
list recapitulates all the different amendments that have been published up to ITU Operational Bulletin No.
1295 of 1.VII.2024.

2.     Recommendation ITU-T Q.708 states that the assignment of signalling area/network codes (SANC) is
to be administered by TSB. Each country will then be responsible for the assignment of international
signalling point codes (ISPC) that will then be notified to TSB.

3.    The numbering plan of Recommendation ITU-T Q.708 contains 2 048 SANCs providing for 16 384
international signalling points. From these, currently 1 536 SANCs are available for assignment allowing for
12 288 international points. At present 1 071 SANCs are assigned; the reported utilization is 6 291
international signalling points.

4.    In order to keep the list up to date, administrations are, therefore, requested to notify TSB, by using
the notification form attached, as soon as an ISPC assignment or withdrawal is made,
www.itu.int/en/ITU-T/inr/forms/Pages/ispc.aspx .

5.    This List will be updated by numbered series of amendments published in the ITU Operational Bulletin.
Furthermore, the information contained in this Annex is also available on the ITU website .

6.    Please address any comments or any modifications concerning this List to the Director of TSB:

             Director of TSB
             International Telecommunication Union
             Place des Nations
             CH-1211 GENEVA 20
             Switzerland
             Tel:         +41 22 730 5211
             Fax:         +41 22 730 5853
             E-mail:      tsbtson@itu.int

7.      The designations employed and the presentation of material in this List do not imply the expression of
any opinion whatsoever on the part of ITU concerning the legal status of any country or geographical area,
or of its authorities.
